[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m656[0m[39m: *[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m657[0m[39m: * On success, the input array describes the type of all arguments and their[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m658[0m[39m: * values.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m659[0m[39m: *[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m660[0m[39m: * The function then iterates over the output segments and outputs them one[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m661[0m[39m: * by one until done. Using the appropriate input arguments [0m[1;39m([0m[39mif any[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m662[0m[39m: *[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m663[0m[39m: * All output is sent to the [0m[32m'stream[0m[32m([0m[32m)[0m[32m'[0m[39m callback, one byte at a time.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m664[0m[39m: *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m665[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m666[0m[39m:static int [0m[1;35mformatf[0m[1;39m([0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m667[0m[39m:  void *userp, [0m[35m/[0m[39m* untouched by [0m[1;35mformat[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, just sent to the [0m[1;35mstream[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m function in[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m668[0m[39m:                  the second argument *[0m[35m/[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m669[0m[39m:  [0m[35m/[0m[39m* function pointer called for each output character *[0m[35m/[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m670[0m[39m:  int [0m[1;39m([0m[39m*stream[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m([0m[39munsigned char, void *[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m,[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m671[0m[39m:  const char *format,    [0m[35m/[0m[39m* %-formatted string *[0m[35m/[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m672[0m[39m:  va_list ap_save[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[35m/[0m[39m* list of parameters *[0m[35m/[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m673[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m674[0m[39m:  static const char nilstr[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m"[0m[32m([0m[32mnil[0m[32m)[0m[32m"[0m[39m;[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m675[0m[39m:  const char *digits = lower_digits;   [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Base-[0m[1;36m36[0m[39m digits for numbers.  *[0m[35m/[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m676[0m[39m:  int done = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;   [0m[35m/[0m[39m* number of characters written  *[0m[35m/[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m677[0m[39m:  int i;[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m678[0m[39m:  int ocount = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; [0m[35m/[0m[39m* number of output segments *[0m[35m/[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m679[0m[39m:  int icount = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; [0m[35m/[0m[39m* number of input arguments *[0m[35m/[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m680[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m681[0m[39m:  struct outsegment output[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mMAX_SEGMENTS[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m682[0m[39m:  struct va_input input[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mMAX_PARAMETERS[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m683[0m[39m:  char work[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mBUFFSIZE[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m684[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m685[0m[39m:  [0m[35m/[0m[39m* [0m[32m'workend'[0m[39m points to the final buffer byte position, but with an extra[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m686[0m[39m:     byte as margin to avoid the [0m[1;39m([0m[39mFALSE?[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m warning Coverity gives us[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m687[0m[39m:     otherwise *[0m[35m/[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m688[0m[39m:  char *workend = &work[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mwork[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m689[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m692[0m[39m:    return [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m696[0m[39m:    struct va_input *iptr;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m194[0m[39m:  char *path;[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m195[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m196[0m[39m:  *done = TRUE; [0m[35m/[0m[39m* unconditionally *[0m[35m/[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m197[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m198[0m[39m:  [0m[35m/[0m[39m* url-decode path before further evaluation *[0m[35m/[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m199[0m[39m:  result = [0m[1;35mCurl_urldecode[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata->state.up.path, [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, &path, NULL, REJECT_CTRL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m200[0m[39m:  [0m[1;35mif[0m[1;39m([0m[39mresult[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m201[0m[39m:    return result;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m202[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m203[0m[39m:    [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Do we need to authenticate? *[0m[35m/[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m204[0m[39m:    user_end = [0m[1;35mstrchr[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpath, [0m[32m'='[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m205[0m[39m:    [0m[35m/[0m[39m* This is an authenticated session *[0m[35m/[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m206[0m[39m:    [0m[1;35mif[0m[1;39m([0m[39muser_end[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m207[0m[39m:      size_t resp_count = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m208[0m[39m:      ssize_t bytes_recv;[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m209[0m[39m:      resp_buf = [0m[1;35mmalloc[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m1024[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m210[0m[39m:      [0m[1;35mmemset[0m[1;39m([0m[39mresp_buf, [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m1024[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m211[0m[39m:      [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Username comes immediately after path *[0m[35m/[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m212[0m[39m:      user_start = [0m[1;35mstrchr[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpath, [0m[32m'/'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m + [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m213[0m[39m:      *user_end = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mchar[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m215[0m[39m:      auth_end = [0m[1;35mstrchr[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpath, [0m[32m'@'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m216[0m[39m:      [0m[1;35mif[0m[1;39m([0m[39mauth_end[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                            [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m218[0m[39m:      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlib/dict.[0m[1;92mc:220[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m232[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m220[0m[39m:      result = [0m[1;35msendf[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata, [0m[32m"CLIENT "[0m[39m LIBCURL_NAME [0m[32m" "[0m[39m LIBCURL_VERSION [0m[32m"\r\n"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m221[0m[39m:      [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m [0m[1;35mwhile[0m[1;39m([0m[39mresult == CURLE_AGAIN[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m222[0m[39m:      [0m[1;35mif[0m[1;39m([0m[39mresult[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m223[0m[39m:        goto error;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m224[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m225[0m[39m:      [0m[1;35mif[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mstrcmp[0m[1;39m([0m[39mauth_start, [0m[32m"debug"[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m226[0m[39m:        do [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m227[0m[39m:        result = [0m[1;35msendf[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata, [0m[32m"Sending extra debug info..."[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m228[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m [0m[1;35mwhile[0m[1;39m([0m[39mresult == CURLE_AGAIN[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m229[0m[39m:        do [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m230[0m[39m:        result = [0m[1;35msendf[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata, user_start[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m231[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m [0m[1;35mwhile[0m[1;39m([0m[39mresult == CURLE_AGAIN[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m232[0m[39m:      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe segmentation fault occurs due to a **format string vulnerability** in the DICT [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprotocol handler at `lib/dict.[0m[1;92mc:230[0m[39m`. The issue arises when user-controlled data [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfrom the URL path is passed directly as a format string to the `[0m[1;35msendf[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` function [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minstead of being treated as data.[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Vulnerability Details[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Critical Location**: `lib/dict.[0m[1;92mc:230[0m[39m`[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresult = [0m[1;35msendf[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata, user_start[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m VULNERABLE[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**How the Crash Occurs**:[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The `user_start` variable is extracted from the URL path [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m212[0m[39m: `user_start [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m= [0m[1;35mstrchr[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpath, [0m[32m'/'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m + [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;`[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. This string contains user-controlled data from the fuzzer input[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. When the fuzzer provides input like `[0m[35m/auth/[0m[39m%s%p%d`, `user_start` points to [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`%s%p%d`[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. This string is passed to `[0m[1;35msendf[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` which treats it as a format string[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. `[0m[1;35msendf[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` calls `[0m[1;35mcurl_mvaprintf[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` → `[0m[1;35mformatf[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` with an empty `va_list` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mno [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39madditional arguments[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. `[0m[1;35mformatf[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` parses the format specifiers [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`%s`, `%p`, `%d`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and attempts to [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maccess arguments from the `va_input` array[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. Since no arguments were provided, the array contains uninitialized memory[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m8[0m[39m. At line [0m[1;36m894[0m[39m in `mprintf.c`, the code dereferences `str` pointer: `else [0m[1;35mif[0m[1;39m([0m[39m*str [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m== [0m[32m'\0'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m9[0m[39m. This `str` pointer contains a [0m[32m"high value address"[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39muninitialized garbage[0m[1;39m)[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m10[0m[39m. Dereferencing this invalid pointer causes the SEGV[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Evidence from Code Analysis[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Correct Pattern** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mused elsewhere in dict.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Line [0m[1;36m324[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m333[0m[39m: `[0m[1;35msendf[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata, [0m[32m"MATCH %s %s %s\r\n"[0m[39m, database, strategy, eword[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Line [0m[1;36m374[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m381[0m[39m: `[0m[1;35msendf[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata, [0m[32m"DEFINE %s %s\r\n"[0m[39m, database, eword[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Incorrect Pattern** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe bug[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Line [0m[1;36m230[0m[39m: `[0m[1;35msendf[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata, user_start[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe correct pattern uses literal format strings with `%s` specifiers for user data,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpreventing format string interpretation.[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Primary Fix: Correct Format String Usage[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location**: `lib/dict.[0m[1;92mc:230[0m[39m`[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Change Required**:[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m BEFORE [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvulnerable[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresult = [0m[1;35msendf[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata, user_start[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m AFTER [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfixed[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresult = [0m[1;35msendf[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata, [0m[32m"%s"[0m[39m, user_start[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This Fix is Optimal[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Minimal Change**: Single-line modification with no functional impact on the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprotocol[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Preserves Functionality**: Still sends the same data to the server, just [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msafely[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Follows Established Pattern**: Aligns with how [0m[1;35msendf[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is used throughout the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcodebase[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **No Side Effects**: Does not affect any other code paths or protocol operations[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Security Best Practice**: Prevents format string vulnerabilities[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Implementation Details[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix should be applied to the initial codebase at `lib/dict.c` line [0m[1;36m230[0m[39m within [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe `[0m[1;35mdict_do[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` function. The change treats `user_start` as data to be formatted [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith `%s` rather than as a format string itself.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Context of the Fix** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m225[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m232[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mif[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mstrcmp[0m[1;39m([0m[39mauth_start, [0m[32m"debug"[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  do [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    result = [0m[1;35msendf[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata, [0m[32m"Sending extra debug info..."[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m [0m[1;35mwhile[0m[1;39m([0m[39mresult == CURLE_AGAIN[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  do [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    result = [0m[1;35msendf[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata, [0m[32m"%s"[0m[39m, user_start[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m FIX APPLIED HERE[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m [0m[1;35mwhile[0m[1;39m([0m[39mresult == CURLE_AGAIN[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why Other Approaches Are Not Needed[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **No mprintf.c Changes**: The crash location in `mprintf.[0m[1;92mc:894[0m[39m` is NOT the root [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcause; it's where the symptom manifests. The formatf function is working as [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdesigned for printf-style formatting.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **No Input Validation**: Adding validation to detect format specifiers in [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muser_start would be redundant and error-prone. The proper fix is to use the correct[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAPI pattern.[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **No Bounds Checking in formatf**: Printf-style functions rely on format strings[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbeing programmer-controlled. Adding runtime bounds checking would break the API [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontract and affect performance.[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **No Changes to Other sendf Calls**: Lines [0m[1;36m220[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m227[0m[39m, and all other sendf calls [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min dict.c already follow the correct pattern.[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Compatibility and Testing[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Preserved Behavior**:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The DICT protocol functionality remains unchanged[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All valid DICT URLs continue to work correctly[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The same data is sent to the server, just safely formatted[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**No Breaking Changes**:[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Existing tests should continue to pass[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fix only affects how user data is passed to formatting functions[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No external API changes[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Fuzzing Support**:[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fix supports the same fuzzing logic[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fuzzer can still test all DICT protocol paths[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Format specifier inputs will now be treated as literal data instead of causing [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcrashes[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Related Code Preservation[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix preserves critical logic:[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- URL parsing and path extraction [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m199[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m218[0m[1;39m)[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Authentication flow [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m206[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m278[0m[1;39m)[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All other protocol commands [0m[1;39m([0m[39mMATCH, DEFINE, etc.[0m[1;39m)[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Error handling and cleanup [0m[1;39m([0m[39merror label[0m[1;39m)[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Security Implications[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis fix addresses a **format string vulnerability** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mCWE-[0m[1;36m134[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m that could [0m          [2m                [0m
